1.Installation of rails:
	command : gem install rails
	
2.Gem : Gems in Rails are libraries that allow any Ruby on Rails developer to add functionalities without writing code.

3.Bundler: provides a constant environment for Ruby projects by tracking and installing suitable gems that are needed.
4.Gem version : for check the current gem verison
	command : gem --version
		  3.2.22

5.rails version : check the rails version 

		command : rails -v
			Rails 6.1.4.1

6.rails new <project_name> : for creating new rails project in local machine .
	command : rails new <project_name>
	
7.rails server: start the server.
	command : rails server
		// your rails server will start automaticaly at localhost : http://127.0.0.1:3000
		
8.rails db:create : for creation of database 
	command : rails db:create
	e
	xample : rails db:create
		 Created database 'simple_cms_development' // database is created

9.Migration generate : to generate the migration for alter the tables.
	command : rails generate migration DoNothingYet
	output:
		  Running via Spring preloader in process 14984
      	          invoke  active_record
      		  create    db/migrate/20211109112006_do_nothing_yet.rb

10.Model (table) : 

rails generate model User first_name:String,last_name:String, email:String
Running via Spring preloader in process 15241
      invoke  active_record
      create    db/migrate/20211109113538_create_users.rb
      create    app/models/user.rb
      invoke    test_unit
      create      test/models/user_test.rb
      create      test/fixtures/users.yml
      
11.Run Migration : to run the migration for creation of the tables.creation of table and updation of table in database.
	command: rails db:migrate
	output:  rails db:migrate
== 20211109113538 CreateUsers: migrating ======================================
-- create_table(:users)
   -> 0.2360s
== 20211109113538 CreateUsers: migrated (0.2362s) =============================

simple_cms_development=# \d users;
                                          Table "public.users"
   Column   |              Type              | Collation | Nullable |              Default              
------------+--------------------------------+-----------+----------+-----------------------------------
 id         | bigint                         |           | not null | nextval('users_id_seq'::regclass)
 last_name  | character varying              |           |          | 
 first_name | character varying              |           |          | 
 email      | character varying              |           |          | 
 created_at | timestamp(6) without time zone |           | not null | 
 updated_at | timestamp(6) without time zone |           | not null | 
Indexes:
    "users_pkey" PRIMARY KEY, btree (id)

12.To see the status of migration :
	command : rails db:migrate:status
	output:
database: simple_cms_development

 Status   Migration ID    Migration Name
--------------------------------------------------
   up     20211109112006  Do nothing yet
   up     20211109113538  Create users

================================================Active Records(DataBase In Rails) Basics=======================================
1.rail console : to start the rail console 
	command : rails c

2.Insertion of data : 
	command :

 user = User.new
 => #<User:0x000056242b2ae180 id: nil, last_name: nil, first_name: nil, email: nil, created_at: nil, updated_at: nil> 
3.0.2 :002 > user.first_name = "kevin"
 => "kevin" 
3.0.2 :003 > user.last_name = "smith"
 => "smith" 
3.0.2 :004 > user.email = "kevin11@gmail.com"
 => "kevin11@gmail.com" 

3.Save the data : update the table 
	command : user.save
	output:
	
3.0.2 :005 > user.save
  TRANSACTION (0.5ms)  BEGIN
  User Create (1.7ms)  INSERT INTO "users" ("last_name", "first_name", "email", "created_at", "updated_at") VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5) RETURNING "id"  [["last_name", "smith"], ["first_name", "kevin"], ["email", "kevin11@gmail.com"], ["created_at", "2021-11-09 12:55:26.151935"], ["updated_at", "2021-11-09 12:55:26.151935"]]
  TRANSACTION (33.8ms)  COMMIT
 => true
